<p class="hide-desktop hide-tablet hide-mobile wp-block-site-tagline">Making developers awesome at machine learning</p>

	<header>
	<h1 class="title entry-title">The Complete Guide to Tool Selection in AI Agents</h1>	</header>
	<div class="mlm-post-meta">
		<div class="post-meta"><span class="small">By</span> <span class="author vcard"><span class="fn"><a href="https://machinelearningmastery.com/author/shittu-olumide/" rel="author">Shittu Olumide</a></span></span> <span class="small">on</span> <abbr title="2026-07-06T21:33:55+1000">July 6, 2026</abbr>   <span class="small">in</span> <span class="categories"><a href="https://machinelearningmastery.com/category/artificial-intelligence/" title="View all items in Artificial Intelligence">Artificial Intelligence</a></span>  <span class="post-comments comments"><a href="https://machinelearningmastery.com/the-complete-guide-to-tool-selection-in-ai-agents/#respond"><i class="fa fa-comment"></i> 0</a></span></div>

</div>
<p>In this article, you will learn why agent accuracy degrades as a tool catalog grows, and six practical techniques for keeping tool selection accurate and efficient at scale.</p>
<p>Topics we will cover include:</p>
<ul>
<li>Why adding more tools to an agent causes tool hallucination and accuracy loss, not just slower responses.</li>
<li>How gating, retrieval, routing, and planning each narrow down what the model sees before it has to choose a tool.</li>
<li>How to build fallback logic and a benchmark harness so you can measure whether any of these fixes actually worked.</li>
</ul>
<p>None of this requires a bigger model, just a smarter view of what the model sees before it acts.</p>
<div style="width: 810px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><a href="https://machinelearningmastery.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/mlm-the-complete-guide-to-tool-selection-in-ai-agents-feature-1.png" target="_blank"><img fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" src="https://machinelearningmastery.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/mlm-the-complete-guide-to-tool-selection-in-ai-agents-feature-1.png" alt="The Complete Guide to Tool Selection in AI Agents" width="800" height="706" /></a><p class="wp-caption-text">The Complete Guide to Tool Selection in AI Agents<br />
<a href="https://machinelearningmastery.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/mlm-the-complete-guide-to-tool-selection-in-ai-agents-feature-1.png" target="_blank">Click to enlarge</a><br /></p></div>
<h2>Introduction</h2>
<p>You build an agent with five tools. It works flawlessly in the demo. Three months later, it has 40 file operations, CRM access, Slack, a calendar, and three different search APIs you bolted on for different teams. The same agent that nailed every demo now calls the wrong tool, hallucinates parameters borrowed from a different tool&#8217;s schema, or stalls mid-task waiting on a call that should never have been made.</p>
<p>Nothing about the model changed. The tool list did. This is not an edge case you&#8217;ll eventually run into. It&#8217;s the default trajectory of every agent that ships and then grows. Research analyzing MCP tool descriptions across the ecosystem has found that a high number contain at least one quality issue, and production benchmarks show agent accuracy degrading measurably once tool counts pass roughly 10 to 15. The <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.03275" target="_blank">RAG-MCP paper</a>, published in May 2025, put hard numbers on the fix: retrieval-based tool selection more than tripled tool selection accuracy from 13.62% to 43.13% while cutting prompt tokens by over half on the same benchmark tasks.</p>
<p>Tool selection isn&#8217;t a minor implementation detail you patch later. It&#8217;s the architectural decision that determines whether an agent survives contact with a real tool catalog. This guide covers six techniques that solve it, in the order you&#8217;d actually deploy them: gating, retrieval, routing, planning, fallback logic, and the benchmark that tells you whether any of it worked.</p>
<h2>Why Tool Selection Breaks at Scale</h2>
<p>Every tool definition — its name, description, and parameter schema — gets sent to the model on every single request, whether that tool gets used or not. With 50-plus tools, this can consume 5 to 7% of the model&#8217;s context before the user&#8217;s actual message arrives, crowding out the conversation history and reasoning space the task actually needs.</p>
<p>The &#8220;<strong>lost in the middle</strong>&#8221; effect compounds this. Models recall information at the start and end of a context window far more reliably than information buried in the middle. With dozens of near-identical tool definitions stacked in sequence, the one tool that&#8217;s actually right for the job often sits exactly in that dead zone, overlooked not because the model can&#8217;t reason about it, but because attention is structurally pulled elsewhere.</p>
<p>The second failure mode is worse: tool hallucination. When an LLM&#8217;s attention spreads across too many similar-sounding tools, it either invents tool names that don&#8217;t exist or calls the correct tool while filling in arguments borrowed from a different tool&#8217;s schema. This is a hard failure. There&#8217;s no &#8220;<strong>slightly wrong</strong>&#8221; way to call a nonexistent function.</p>
<p>OpenAI documents a <a href="https://community.openai.com/t/maximum-amount-of-tools-for-the-bot-to-use/665720" target="_blank">hard ceiling of 128 tools per agent</a>, but real degradation shows up well before that limit; most production teams see accuracy drop noticeably once they cross 15 to 20 tools in active rotation. The fix isn&#8217;t a bigger context window. It&#8217;s controlling what the model sees in the first place.</p>
<h2>Gating: Deciding Whether a Tool Is Needed at All</h2>
<p>Before you optimize which tool to pick, ask a cheaper question first: does this turn need a tool at all? A meaningful fraction of agent turns are purely conversational: &#8220;<strong>thanks</strong>,&#8221; &#8220;<strong>what do you mean by that</strong>,&#8221; a follow-up clarification. Running full retrieval and tool-selection reasoning on every single turn means paying the full agentic overhead even when the answer is &#8220;<strong>no tool needed</strong>.&#8221;</p>
<p>A gate is a fast, cheap classifier — sometimes a small model call, sometimes just pattern matching — that runs before anything expensive does.</p>
<p></p>
		<div id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-syntax crayon-theme-classic urvanov-syntax-highlighter-font-monaco urvanov-syntax-highlighter-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" touchscreen minimize scroll-mouseover disable-anim" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings="" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><span class="crayon-title"></span>
			<div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-expand-button" title="Expand Code"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-copy-button" title="Copy"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div></div></div>
			<div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div>
			<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain-wrap"><textarea wrap="soft" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick"  style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
# gate.py
# Prerequisites: none beyond Python's standard library (re)
# Run: python gate.py

import re

CONVERSATIONAL_PATTERNS = [
    r"^\s*(thanks|thank you|thx|ok|okay|cool|got it|sounds good|sure|great)\b",
    r"^\s*(hi|hello|hey|good morning|good evening)\b",
    r"^\s*what do you mean\b",
    r"^\s*can you (clarify|explain that)\b",
]

ACTION_KEYWORDS = [
    "send", "create", "search", "find", "look up", "schedule", "book",
    "read", "write", "query", "summarize", "translate", "check",
]

def gate(query: str) -&gt; dict:
    """
    Cheap pre-filter that decides whether the full tool-selection pipeline
    needs to run at all. Short-circuits conversational turns before
    retrieval, routing, or planning ever fires.
    """
    q_lower = query.strip().lower()

    # Tier 1: regex match against known conversational patterns -- near-zero cost
    for pattern in CONVERSATIONAL_PATTERNS:
        if re.match(pattern, q_lower):
            return {"tool_needed": False, "reason": "conversational_pattern", "tier": 1}

    # Tier 2: if there's no action verb and the message is short, likely no tool needed
    has_action_keyword = any(kw in q_lower for kw in ACTION_KEYWORDS)
    if not has_action_keyword and len(q_lower.split()) &lt; 5:
        return {"tool_needed": False, "reason": "short_with_no_action_keyword", "tier": 2}

    return {"tool_needed": True, "reason": "action_keyword_or_long_query", "tier": 2}


if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_queries = [
        "thanks!",
        "What's the weather like in Lagos today?",
        "ok",
        "Can you send an email to the sales team about the delay?",
    ]
    for q in test_queries:
        result = gate(q)
        print(f"'{q}' -&gt; tool_needed={result['tool_needed']} ({result['reason']})")</textarea></div>

class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-40">40</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-41">41</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-42">42</div><div 				</td>
						<td class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-code"><div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-1"><span class="crayon-p"># gate.py</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-2"><span class="crayon-p"># Prerequisites: none beyond Python's standard library (re)</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-3"><span class="crayon-p"># Run: python gate.py</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-4">&nbsp;</div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-5"><span class="crayon-e">import </span><span class="crayon-e">re</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-6">&nbsp;</div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-7"><span class="crayon-v">CONVERSATIONAL_PATTERNS</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-8"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-i">r</span><span class="crayon-s">"^\s*(thanks|thank you|thx|ok|okay|cool|got it|sounds good|sure|great)\b"</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-9"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span mean\b"</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-11"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span the full tool-selection pipeline</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-22"><span class="crayon-s">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;needs Short-circuits conversational turns before</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-23"><span class="crayon-s">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;retrieval, routing, or planning ever fires.</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-24"><span class="crayon-s">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</span><span class="crayon-s">""</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-25"><span id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-26">&nbsp;</div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-27"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-p"># Tier 1: regex match against known conversational patterns -- near-zero cost</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-28"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-st">for</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-e">pattern </span><span class="crayon-st">in</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">CONVERSATIONAL_PATTERNS</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-29"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-st">if</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">re</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-e">match</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-v">pattern</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">q_lower</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-30"><span class="crayon-s">"conversational_pattern"</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-s">"tier"</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span><span action verb and the message is short, likely no tool needed</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-33"><span class="crayon-e">has_action_keyword </span><span class="crayon-st">and</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-e">len</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-v">q_lower</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-e">split</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">&lt;</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">5</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-35"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-st">return</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">{</span><span class="crayon-s">"tool_needed"</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-t">False</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-s">"reason"</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-s">"short_with_no_action_keyword"</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-s">"tier"</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">2</span><span class="crayon-sy">}</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-36">&nbsp;</div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-37"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-st">return</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">{</span><span class="crayon-s">"tool_needed"</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-t">True</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-s">"reason"</span><span class="crayon-s">"tier"</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">2</span><span class="crayon-sy">}</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-38">&nbsp;</div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-39">&nbsp;</div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-40"><span class="crayon-st">if</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">__name__</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">==</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-s">"__main__"</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-41"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-42"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-s">"thanks!"</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-43"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-s">"What's the weather like in Lagos today?"</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-44"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-s">"ok"</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-45"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-s">"Can you send an email to the sales team about the delay?"</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-46"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-47"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-v">result</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-e">gate</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-v">q</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac526714013209-49"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-e">print</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-i">f</span><span class="crayon-s">"'{q}' -&gt; tool_needed={result['tool_needed']} ({result['reason']})"</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div><p></p>
<p>How to run (no dependencies required):</p>
<p></p>
		<div id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac532481523750" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-syntax crayon-theme-classic urvanov-syntax-highlighter-font-monaco urvanov-syntax-highlighter-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" touchscreen minimize scroll-mouseover disable-anim" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings="" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><span class="crayon-title"></span>
			<div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-expand-button" title="Expand Code"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-copy-button" title="Copy"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div></div></div>

python gate.py</textarea></div>
			<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-main" style="">
				<table class="crayon-table">
					<tr class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-row">
				<td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="show">
					<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-nums-content" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"><div class="crayon-num" data-line="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac532481523750-1">1</div></div>
				</td>
						<td class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-code"><div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac532481523750-1"><span class="crayon-e">python </span><span class="crayon-v">gate</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-v">py</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div><p></p>
<p>This costs almost nothing and catches a meaningful share of turns before they reach the expensive part of the pipeline. The threshold for &#8220;is this worth building&#8221; is low: if even 20–30% of your turns are conversational, gating pays for itself immediately in both latency and token cost.</p>
<h2>Retrieval-Based Tool Selection</h2>
<p>This is the technique with the strongest published evidence behind it. Instead of sending every tool definition on every call, you index tool descriptions in a vector store, embed the incoming query, retrieve only the top-K most relevant tools, and send just those to the model.</p>
<p>The <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.03275" target="_blank">RAG-MCP framework</a> is the reference implementation of this idea, using semantic retrieval to identify the most relevant MCP tools for a query before the LLM ever sees the full catalog. The reported numbers are not subtle: tool selection accuracy rose from 13.62% with the full catalog exposed to 43.13% with retrieval-filtered selection, more than tripling accuracy, while cutting prompt tokens by over 50% on the same benchmark tasks.</p>
<p></p>
		<div id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac537020841426" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-syntax crayon-theme-classic urvanov-syntax-highlighter-font-monaco urvanov-syntax-highlighter-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" touchscreen minimize scroll-mouseover disable-anim" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings="" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><span class="crayon-title"></span>
			<div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-expand-button" title="Expand Code"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-copy-button" title="Copy"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div></div></div>
			<div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div>
			<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain-wrap"><textarea wrap="soft" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick"  style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
# retriever.py
# Prerequisites: pip install sentence-transformers faiss-cpu numpy
# Run: python retriever.py

import numpy as np
from sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer
import faiss

TOOL_CATALOG = [
    {"name": "search_web", "description": "Search the web for current information on any topic"},
    {"name": "read_file", "description": "Read the contents of a file given its path"},
    {"name": "write_file", "description": "Write or overwrite content to a file at a given path"},
    {"name": "send_email", "description": "Send an email to a recipient with subject and body"},
    {"name": "create_calendar_event", "description": "Create a new calendar event with a title, date, and time"},
    {"name": "query_database", "description": "Run a SQL query against the company database"},
    {"name": "list_github_issues", "description": "List open issues in a GitHub repository"},
    {"name": "create_github_pr", "description": "Create a pull request on a GitHub repository"},
    {"name": "send_slack_message", "description": "Send a message to a Slack channel or user"},
    {"name": "get_weather", "description": "Get current weather conditions for a city"},
    {"name": "translate_text", "description": "Translate text from one language to another"},
    {"name": "summarize_document", "description": "Summarize a long document into key points"},
    {"name": "lookup_stock_price", "description": "Get the current stock price for a ticker symbol"},
    {"name": "book_flight", "description": "Search and book a flight between two cities"},
    {"name": "create_invoice", "description": "Generate an invoice for a customer with line items"},
]

class ToolRetriever:
    """
    Embeds tool descriptions once at startup and indexes them in FAISS.
    At runtime, embeds the incoming query and returns only the top-K
    most relevant tools -- not the full catalog.
    """
    def __init__(self, tools: list[dict], model_name: str = "all-MiniLM-L6-v2"):
        self.tools = tools
        self.model = SentenceTransformer(model_name)
        descriptions = [f"{t['name']}: {t['description']}" for t in tools]
        embeddings = self.model.encode(descriptions, normalize_embeddings=True)
        # IndexFlatIP = inner product search, which equals cosine similarity
        # when vectors are normalized -- the standard setup for this use case.
        self.index = faiss.IndexFlatIP(embeddings.shape[1])
        self.index.add(np.array(embeddings, dtype=np.float32))

    def retrieve(self, query: str, top_k: int = 3) -&gt; list[dict]:
        query_emb = self.model.encode([query], normalize_embeddings=True)
        scores, indices = self.index.search(np.array(query_emb, dtype=np.float32), top_k)
        return [
            {**self.tools[idx], "score": float(score)}
            for score, idx in zip(scores[0], indices[0])
        ]


if __name__ == "__main__":
    retriever = ToolRetriever(TOOL_CATALOG)

    queries = [
        "What's the weather like in Lagos today?",
        "Can you check if there are any open bugs in our repo?",
        "Send a message to the engineering channel about the deploy",
    ]
    for q in queries:
        results = retriever.retrieve(q, top_k=3)
        print(f"\nQuery: '{q}'")
        for r in results:
            print(f"  {r['name']} (score={r['score']:.3f})")</textarea></div>

class="crayon-o">:</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac537020841426-64"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-e">print</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-i">f</span><span class="crayon-s">"&nbsp;&nbsp;{r['name']} (score={r['score']:.3f})"</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div><p></p>
<p>How to run:</p>
<p></p>
		<div id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac53e621894581" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-syntax crayon-theme-classic urvanov-syntax-highlighter-font-monaco urvanov-syntax-highlighter-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" touchscreen minimize scroll-mouseover disable-anim" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">

pip install sentence-transformers faiss-cpu numpy
python retriever.py</textarea></div>

				<td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="show">

					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div><p></p>
<p>Only the top-3 tools out of a 15-tool catalog get sent to the model per query, an 80% reduction in tool definitions on every call, and the accuracy lift compounds because the model is now choosing between a handful of genuinely relevant candidates instead of scanning past a dozen near-misses.</p>
<h2>Semantic Routing</h2>
<p>Routing is retrieval&#8217;s lighter cousin, and it fits a different shape of problem. Retrieval answers &#8220;<strong>which specific tool</strong>&#8221; out of a flat list. Routing answers &#8220;<strong>which toolbox</strong>&#8221; — useful when your tools cluster naturally into categories (data, communication, scheduling) and you want to load only the relevant category&#8217;s tools rather than re-ranking the entire catalog every time.</p>
<p></p>
		<div id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac542156931586" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-syntax crayon-theme-classic urvanov-syntax-highlighter-font-monaco urvanov-syntax-highlighter-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" touchscreen minimize scroll-mouseover disable-anim" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings="" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><span class="crayon-title"></span>
			<div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-expand-button" title="Expand Code"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-copy-button" title="Copy"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div></div></div>
			<div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div>
			<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain-wrap"><textarea wrap="soft" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick"  style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
# router.py
# Prerequisites: pip install scikit-learn numpy
# Run: python router.py

import numpy as np
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity

CATEGORIES = {
    "data":          ["query the database", "read a file", "write data to storage", "run a SQL query"],
    "communication": ["send an email", "post a slack message", "notify the team", "send a message"],
    "scheduling":    ["create a calendar event", "book a meeting", "schedule an appointment"],
}

class SemanticRouter:
    """
    Routes a query to a tool category using similarity against category
    centroid embeddings. Falls back to 'general' when no category clears
    the confidence threshold -- never guesses on a low-confidence match.
    """
    def __init__(self, categories: dict[str, list[str]], confidence_threshold: float = 0.15):
        self.threshold = confidence_threshold
        self.vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
        all_examples = [ex for exs in categories.values() for ex in exs]
        self.vectorizer.fit(all_examples)

        # Build one centroid vector per category by averaging its example embeddings
        self.centroids = {}
        for cat, examples in categories.items():
            vecs = self.vectorizer.transform(examples).toarray()
            self.centroids[cat] = vecs.mean(axis=0)

    def route(self, query: str) -&gt; dict:
        query_vec = self.vectorizer.transform([query]).toarray()[0]
        scores = {
            cat: float(cosine_similarity([query_vec], [centroid])[0][0])
            for cat, centroid in self.centroids.items()
        }
        best_cat   = max(scores, key=scores.get)
        best_score = scores[best_cat]

        if best_score &lt; self.threshold:
            return {"category": "general", "confidence": best_score}

        return {"category": best_cat, "confidence": best_score}


if __name__ == "__main__":
    router = SemanticRouter(CATEGORIES)

    test_queries = [
        "Can you post a message in the sales Slack channel?",
        "I need to run a query against our production database",
        "Schedule a meeting with the design team for tomorrow",
        "asdkj qpwoe zxcv nonsense",
    ]
    for q in test_queries:
        result = router.route(q)
        print(f"'{q}' -&gt; {result['category']} (confidence={result['confidence']:.3f})")</textarea></div>
			<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-main" style="">
				<table class="crayon-table">
					<tr class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-row">
				<td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="show">
					<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-nums-content" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"><div class="crayon-num" class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac542156931586-17"><span class="crayon-s">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Routes a query to a tool category using similarity against category</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac542156931586-18"><span class="crayon-s">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;centroid embeddings. <p>How to run:</p>

				<td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="show">

						<td class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-code"><div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac548201010587-1"><span class="crayon-e">pip </span><span class="crayon-e">install </span><span class="crayon-v">scikit</span><span class="crayon-o">-</span><span class="crayon-e">learn </span><span class="crayon-e">numpy</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac548201010587-2"><span class="crayon-e">python </span><span class="crayon-v">router</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-v">py</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div><p></p>
<p>The fallback to &#8220;<strong>general</strong>&#8221; on the gibberish query matters as much as the correct routes do. A router that always picks something, even on a query it has no real signal for, is more dangerous than one that admits it doesn&#8217;t know.</p>
<h2>Planner-Based Tool Selection</h2>
<p>Retrieval and routing both answer &#8220;<strong>what&#8217;s relevant to this single turn</strong>.&#8221; Multi-step tasks need something different: a sequence of tool calls planned upfront, with each step scoped to only the tools it specifically needs. This is the architecture that avoids what&#8217;s sometimes called the God Agent anti-pattern — a single agent holding 20 tools in context with no plan structure — where a failure anywhere corrupts the whole task.</p>
<p><strong>The pattern</strong>: ask the model to output a structured plan first, an ordered list of subtasks, each tagged with the capability it requires, before any tool executes. Then retrieve tools per step, scoped to that step&#8217;s tag.</p>
<p></p>
		<div id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac54c689862737" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-syntax crayon-theme-classic urvanov-syntax-highlighter-font-monaco urvanov-syntax-highlighter-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" touchscreen minimize scroll-mouseover disable-anim" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings="" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><span class="crayon-title"></span>
			<div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-expand-button" title="Expand Code"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-copy-button" title="Copy"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div></div></div>
			<div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div>
			<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain-wrap"><textarea wrap="soft" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick"  style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
# planner.py
# Prerequisites: none beyond Python's standard library (json)
# Run: python planner.py

import json
from dataclasses import dataclass

@dataclass
class PlanStep:
    step_number: int
    description: str
    required_capability: str

def parse_plan(raw_plan_json: str) -&gt; list[PlanStep]:
    """Parse a planner LLM's JSON output into structured PlanStep objects."""
    data = json.loads(raw_plan_json)
    return [
        PlanStep(s["step_number"], s["description"], s["required_capability"])
        for s in data["steps"]
    ]

# Capability -&gt; tool-name mapping. In production this feeds the retriever
# from the previous section, scoped to only the tools tagged for this capability.
CAPABILITY_TOOLS = {
    "search":        ["search_web", "query_database"],
    "file_io":       ["read_file", "write_file"],
    "communication": ["send_email", "send_slack_message"],
    "synthesis":     ["summarize_document"],
}

def get_scoped_tools(step: PlanStep) -&gt; list[str]:
    """Return only the tools relevant to this step -- not the full catalog."""
    return CAPABILITY_TOOLS.get(step.required_capability, [])


if __name__ == "__main__":
    # This JSON would normally come from an LLM call asking it to decompose
    # the task into steps, each tagged with the capability it needs.
    mock_plan = json.dumps({
        "steps": [
            {"step_number": 1, "description": "Search for the latest sales report file", "required_capability": "search"},
            {"step_number": 2, "description": "Read the contents of the report file", "required_capability": "file_io"},
            {"step_number": 3, "description": "Summarize the key findings", "required_capability": "synthesis"},
            {"step_number": 4, "description": "Email the summary to the sales lead", "required_capability": "communication"},
        ]
    })

    plan = parse_plan(mock_plan)
    for step in plan:
        scoped = get_scoped_tools(step)
        print(f"Step {step.step_number}: {step.description}")
        print(f"  Capability: {step.required_capability} -&gt; tools available: {scoped}")</textarea></div>

id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac54c689862737-25"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-s">"search"</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-s">"search_web"</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-s">"query_database"</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac54c689862737-26"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-s">"file_io"</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-s">"read_file"</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-s">"write_file"</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac54c689862737-27"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-s">"communication"</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span><span JSON would normally come from an LLM call asking it to decompose</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac54c689862737-38"><span </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-e">parse_plan</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-v">mock_plan</span><span <p>How to run (no dependencies required):</p>

<p>Each step in this example sees one or two tools, never the full set. That&#8217;s the actual mechanism behind why planning helps: it&#8217;s not that the model reasons better when it has a plan; it&#8217;s that the plan lets you legitimately narrow the tool list per step, which is the same lever retrieval pulls, applied at a finer grain.</p>
<h2>Fallback Logic</h2>
<p>Retrieval and routing both fail sometimes, not because the architecture is wrong, but because real queries are ambiguous, underspecified, or genuinely outside the tool catalog&#8217;s coverage. What you do when the top match&#8217;s confidence is low determines whether your agent degrades gracefully or starts guessing.</p>
<p>A three-tier fallback chain handles this without resorting to a try/except that just crashes the conversation: resolve directly when confidence is high, retry with a reformulated query when it isn&#8217;t, and escalate to an explicit clarification request rather than forcing a tool call when even the retry comes up short.</p>
<p></p>
		<div id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-syntax crayon-theme-classic urvanov-syntax-highlighter-font-monaco urvanov-syntax-highlighter-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" touchscreen minimize scroll-mouseover disable-anim" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings="" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><span class="crayon-title"></span>
			<div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-expand-button" title="Expand Code"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-copy-button" title="Copy"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div></div></div>
			<div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div>
			<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain-wrap"><textarea wrap="soft" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick"  style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
# fallback.py
# Prerequisites: pip install scikit-learn numpy
# Run: python fallback.py

import numpy as np
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity

TOOL_CATALOG = [
    {"name": "search_web", "description": "Search the web for current information on any topic"},
    {"name": "get_weather", "description": "Get the current weather forecast for a city"},
    {"name": "send_email", "description": "Send an email to a recipient with subject and body"},
    {"name": "list_github_issues", "description": "List open issues and bugs in a GitHub repository"},
]

class RetrieverWithFallback:
    """
    Wraps retrieval with a three-tier fallback chain:
    1. High confidence  -&gt; use the top result directly
    2. Low confidence   -&gt; retry with a reformulated query
    3. Still low        -&gt; escalate to a clarification request, never guess
    """
    def __init__(self, tools, confidence_threshold: float = 0.12):
        self.tools = tools
        self.threshold = confidence_threshold
        self.vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
        descs = [f"{t['name']}: {t['description']}" for t in tools]
        self.tool_vectors = self.vectorizer.fit_transform(descs)

    def _raw_retrieve(self, query: str):
        query_vec = self.vectorizer.transform([query])
        sims = cosine_similarity(query_vec, self.tool_vectors)[0]
        top_idx = int(np.argmax(sims))
        return self.tools[top_idx], float(sims[top_idx])

    def retrieve_with_fallback(self, query: str) -&gt; dict:
        tool, score = self._raw_retrieve(query)
        if score &gt;= self.threshold:
            return {"status": "resolved", "tool": tool["name"], "confidence": score, "attempts": 1}

        # Reformulate by stripping filler words. In production, this step would
        # be an LLM call asking it to restate the query in terms of intent/capability.
        reformulated = query.replace("can you", "").replace("please", "").replace("?", "").strip()
        tool2, score2 = self._raw_retrieve(reformulated)
        if score2 &gt;= self.threshold:
            return {"status": "resolved", "tool": tool2["name"], "confidence": score2, "attempts": 2}

        return {
            "status": "escalated", "tool": None,
            "confidence": max(score, score2), "attempts": 2,
            "clarification_request": (
                f"I'm not confident which tool fits '{query}'. "
                f"Could you clarify what you'd like me to do?"
            ),
        }


if __name__ == "__main__":
    retriever = RetrieverWithFallback(TOOL_CATALOG)

    for q in ["What's the weather forecast in Lagos?", "xyzzy plugh random nonsense"]:
        result = retriever.retrieve_with_fallback(q)
        print(f"Query: '{q}'")
        print(f"  Status: {result['status']}")
        if result["status"] == "resolved":
            print(f"  Tool: {result['tool']} (confidence={result['confidence']:.3f})")
        else:
            print(f"  {result['clarification_request']}")</textarea></div>
			<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-main" style="">
				<table class="crayon-table">
					<tr class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-row">
				<td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="show">
					<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-nums-content" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"><div class="crayon-num" data-line="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-1">1</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-2">2</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-3">3</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-4">4</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-5">5</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-6">6</div><div class="crayon-num" data-line="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-7">7</div><div </span><span class="crayon-e">cosine_similarity</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-8">&nbsp;</div><div class="crayon-line" for current information on any topic"</span><span class="crayon-sy">}</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span></div><div class="crayon-line" class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-sy">{</span><span class="crayon-s">"name"</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-s">"send_email"</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-s">"description"</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-s">"Send an email to a recipient with subject and body"</span><span class="crayon-sy">}</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-13"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-sy">{</span><span class="crayon-s">"name"</span><span id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-16"><span class="crayon-t">class</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">RetrieverWithFallback</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-17"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-s">""</span><span class="crayon-s">"</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-18"><span class="crayon-s">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Wraps retrieval with a three-tier fallback chain:</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-19"><span class="crayon-s">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1. High confidence&nbsp;&nbsp;-&gt; use the top result directly</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-20"><span class="crayon-s">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2. Low confidence&nbsp;&nbsp; -&gt; retry with a reformulated query</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-21"><span class="crayon-s">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3. Still low&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;-&gt; escalate to a clarification request, never guess</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-22"><span class="crayon-s">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</span><span class="crayon-s">""</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-23"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-e">def </span><span class="crayon-e">__init__</span><span </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">0.12</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-24"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-r">self</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-v">tools</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-e">tools</span></div><div class="crayon-v">descs</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-i">f</span><span class="crayon-s">"{t['name']}: {t['description']}"</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-st">for</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-i">t</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-st">in</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">tools</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-28"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-r">self</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-v">tool_vectors</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-r">self</span><span crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-30"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-e">def </span><span class="crayon-e">_raw_retrieve</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-r">self</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">query</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">str</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span><span class="crayon-o">:</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-31"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-v">query_vec</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-r">self</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-v">vectorizer</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-32"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-v">sims</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-e">cosine_similarity</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-v">query_vec</span><span class="crayon-sy">,</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-r">self</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-v">tool_vectors</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-cn">0</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-33"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-v">top_idx</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-t">int</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-v">np</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-e">argmax</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-v">sims</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac55b720315454-34"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-st">return</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-r">self</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-v">tools</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-v">top_idx</span><span <p>How to run:</p>
<p></p>
		<div id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac561303562517" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-syntax crayon-theme-classic urvanov-syntax-highlighter-font-monaco urvanov-syntax-highlighter-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" touchscreen minimize scroll-mouseover disable-anim" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">

pip install scikit-learn numpy
python fallback.py</textarea></div>

				</table>
			</div>
		</div><p></p>
<p>The escalation path is the one most teams skip when they first build this, and it&#8217;s the one that matters most in production. A confidently wrong tool call is worse than a system that asks, &#8220;<strong>I&#8217;m not sure, could you clarify?</strong>&#8221; The second failure mode is recoverable in one turn. The first one usually isn&#8217;t.</p>
<h2>Benchmarking Your Tool Selection System</h2>
<p>Everything above is a hypothesis until you measure it. The methodology is straightforward: build a labeled set of (query, correct tool) pairs, run your pipeline against it, and measure accuracy, token cost, and latency, comparing your filtered pipeline against the naive full-catalog baseline. <a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2508.07575" target="_blank">MCPToolBench++</a>, a large-scale benchmark built from over 4,000 real MCP servers across 40-plus categories, is the reference for how rigorously this should be structured at scale, but the core idea works at any size.</p>
<p></p>
		<div id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac568575579264" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-syntax crayon-theme-classic urvanov-syntax-highlighter-font-monaco urvanov-syntax-highlighter-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" touchscreen minimize scroll-mouseover disable-anim" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings="" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><span class="crayon-title"></span>

			<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain-wrap"><textarea wrap="soft" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick"  style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
# benchmark.py
# Prerequisites: pip install scikit-learn numpy
# Run: python benchmark.py

import time
import numpy as np
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity

TOOL_CATALOG = [
    {"name": "search_web", "description": "Search the web for current information on any topic"},
    {"name": "read_file", "description": "Read the contents of a file given its path"},
    {"name": "write_file", "description": "Write or overwrite content to a file at a given path"},
    {"name": "send_email", "description": "Send an email to a recipient with subject and body"},
    {"name": "create_calendar_event", "description": "Create a new calendar event with a title and time"},
    {"name": "query_database", "description": "Run a SQL query against the company database"},
    {"name": "list_github_issues", "description": "List open issues and bugs in a GitHub repository"},
    {"name": "send_slack_message", "description": "Send a message to a Slack channel or user"},
    {"name": "get_weather", "description": "Get current weather conditions for a city"},
    {"name": "book_flight", "description": "Search and book a flight between two cities"},
]

# Labeled benchmark set: (query, expected_tool). Build yours from real
# logged queries once you have production traffic -- this is a seed set.
BENCHMARK_SET = [
    ("What's the weather in Abuja right now?", "get_weather"),
    ("Send an email to the finance team", "send_email"),
    ("List the open issues on our main repo", "list_github_issues"),
    ("Book me a flight from Lagos to London", "book_flight"),
    ("Query the database for last week's signups", "query_database"),
    ("Post an update in the team Slack channel", "send_slack_message"),
    ("Search the web for the latest interest rates", "search_web"),
    ("Read the contents of config.yaml", "read_file"),
]

def estimate_tokens(text: str) -&gt; int:
    """Rough token estimate (1 token ~ 4 characters) -- good enough for relative comparison."""
    return len(text) // 4

class BenchmarkHarness:
    """Runs a labeled query set through a retriever and reports accuracy, token cost, and latency."""

    def __init__(self, tools: list[dict], top_k: int = 3):
        self.tools = tools
        self.top_k = top_k
        self.vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
        descs = [f"{t['name']}: {t['description']}" for t in tools]
        self.tool_vectors = self.vectorizer.fit_transform(descs)
        self.full_catalog_tokens = sum(estimate_tokens(d) for d in descs)

    def _retrieve(self, query: str, top_k: int) -&gt; list[dict]:
        query_vec = self.vectorizer.transform([query])
        sims = cosine_similarity(query_vec, self.tool_vectors)[0]
        top_indices = np.argsort(sims)[::-1][:top_k]
        return [self.tools[i] for i in top_indices]

    def run(self, benchmark_set: list[tuple], use_retrieval: bool = True) -&gt; dict:
        correct, total_tokens, latencies = 0, 0, []

        for query, expected_tool in benchmark_set:
            t0 = time.perf_counter()

            if use_retrieval:
                candidates = self._retrieve(query, top_k=self.top_k)
                tokens_this_query = sum(
                    estimate_tokens(f"{t['name']}: {t['description']}") for t in candidates
                )
            else:
                # Baseline: send the full, unfiltered catalog every time
                candidates = self.tools
                tokens_this_query = self.full_catalog_tokens

            if expected_tool in [c["name"] for c in candidates]:
                correct += 1
            total_tokens += tokens_this_query
            latencies.append(time.perf_counter() - t0)

        n = len(benchmark_set)
        latencies_sorted = sorted(latencies)
        return {
            "accuracy":       round(correct / n, 4),
            "avg_tokens":     round(total_tokens / n, 1),
            "p50_latency_ms": round(latencies_sorted[len(latencies_sorted) // 2] * 1000, 3),
            "p95_latency_ms": round(latencies_sorted[int(len(latencies_sorted) * 0.95)] * 1000, 3),
        }


if __name__ == "__main__":
    harness = BenchmarkHarness(TOOL_CATALOG, top_k=3)

    baseline  = harness.run(BENCHMARK_SET, use_retrieval=False)
    retrieval = harness.run(BENCHMARK_SET, use_retrieval=True)

    print("Baseline (full catalog every time):")
    print(f"  Accuracy:         {baseline['accuracy']*100:.1f}%")
    print(f"  Avg tokens/query: {baseline['avg_tokens']}")

    print("\nRetrieval-filtered (top-3):")
    print(f"  Accuracy:         {retrieval['accuracy']*100:.1f}%")
    print(f"  Avg tokens/query: {retrieval['avg_tokens']}")

    reduction = (1 - retrieval["avg_tokens"] / baseline["avg_tokens"]) * 100
    print(f"\nToken reduction with retrieval: {reduction:.1f}%")</textarea></div>

class="crayon-i">f</span><span class="crayon-s">"&nbsp;&nbsp;Accuracy:&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; {retrieval['accuracy']*100:.1f}%"</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac568575579264-100"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-e">print</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-i">f</span><span class="crayon-s">"&nbsp;&nbsp;Avg tokens/query: {retrieval['avg_tokens']}"</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac568575579264-101">&nbsp;</div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac568575579264-102"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-v">reduction</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">=</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-cn">1</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">-</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">retrieval</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-s">"avg_tokens"</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">/</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-v">baseline</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-s">"avg_tokens"</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-o">*</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span><span class="crayon-cn">100</span></div><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac568575579264-103"><span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-e">print</span><span class="crayon-sy">(</span><span class="crayon-i">f</span><span class="crayon-s">"\nToken reduction with retrieval: {reduction:.1f}%"</span><span class="crayon-sy">)</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div><p></p>
<p>How to run:</p>
<p></p>
		<div id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac58a125406278" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-syntax crayon-theme-classic urvanov-syntax-highlighter-font-monaco urvanov-syntax-highlighter-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" touchscreen minimize scroll-mouseover disable-anim" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings="" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><span class="crayon-title"></span>
			<div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-expand-button" title="Expand Code"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-copy-button" title="Copy"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button urvanov-syntax-highlighter-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window"><div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-button-icon"></div></div></div></div>
			<div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div>
			<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain-wrap"><textarea wrap="soft" class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick"  style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
pip install scikit-learn numpy
python benchmark.py</textarea></div>
			<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-main" style="">
				<table class="crayon-table">
					<tr class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-row">
				<td class="crayon-nums " data-settings="show">
					<div class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-nums-content" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"><div class="crayon-num" data-line="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac58a125406278-1">1</div><div class="crayon-num crayon-striped-num" data-line="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac58a125406278-2">2</div></div>
				</td>
						<td class="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-code"><div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><div class="crayon-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac58a125406278-1"><span class="crayon-e">pip </span><span class="crayon-e">install </span><span class="crayon-v">scikit</span><span class="crayon-o">-</span><span class="crayon-e">learn </span><span class="crayon-e">numpy</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="urvanov-syntax-highlighter-6a4c324aac58a125406278-2"><span class="crayon-e">python </span><span class="crayon-v">benchmark</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-v">py</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div><p></p>
<p>On this 10-tool catalog with an 8-query benchmark set, retrieval-filtering held accuracy steady while cutting average tokens per query by roughly 70%. The exact numbers will shift with your catalog and query set, but the comparison structure is what matters: you now have a repeatable way to answer &#8220;did this change actually help&#8221; instead of relying on a handful of manual spot checks.</p>
<h2>Wrapping up</h2>
<p>These six techniques aren&#8217;t competing options; they&#8217;re layers. Gating filters out turns that need no tool at all, cheaply, before anything else runs. Retrieval or routing narrows the catalog down to what&#8217;s actually relevant for the turns that remain. Planning sequences of multi-step tasks so each step only sees the tools it needs. Fallback logic catches the cases where the first attempt doesn&#8217;t land cleanly. Benchmarking is how you know whether any of the above made a measurable difference, rather than just feeling better.</p>
<p>The RAG-MCP result, with accuracy more than tripling and tokens cut by half, isn&#8217;t an outlier. It&#8217;s what happens predictably once you stop asking a model to read through a full phone book before every decision. None of these techniques requires a bigger model or a longer context window. They require treating the tool list itself as something to be designed, not just appended to.</p>
<p><strong>Resources</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.03275" target="_blank">RAG-MCP: Mitigating Prompt Bloat in LLM Tool Selection via Retrieval-Augmented Generation</a></li>
<li><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2508.07575" target="_blank">MCPToolBench++: A Large-Scale MCP Tool Use Benchmark</a></li>
</ul>

</script><script type="text/javascript">
		/* MonsterInsights Scroll Tracking */
		if ( typeof(jQuery) !== 'undefined' ) {
		jQuery( document ).ready(function(){
		function monsterinsights_scroll_tracking_load() {
		if ( ( typeof(__gaTracker) !== 'undefined' && __gaTracker && __gaTracker.hasOwnProperty( "loaded" ) && __gaTracker.loaded == true ) || ( typeof(__gtagTracker) !== 'undefined' && __gtagTracker ) ) {
		(function(factory) {
		factory(jQuery);
		}(function($) {

		/* Scroll Depth */
		"use strict";
		var defaults = {
		percentage: true
		};

		var $window = $(window),
		cache = [],
		scrollEventBound = false,
		lastPixelDepth = 0;

		/*
		* Plugin
		*/

		$.scrollDepth = function(options) {

		var startTime = +new Date();

		options = $.extend({}, defaults, options);

		/*
		* Functions
		*/

		function sendEvent(action, label, scrollDistance, timing) {
		if ( 'undefined' === typeof MonsterInsightsObject || 'undefined' === typeof MonsterInsightsObject.sendEvent ) {
		return;
		}
			var paramName = action.toLowerCase();
	var fieldsArray = {
	send_to: 'G-JZP3DWZZ8W',
	non_interaction: true
	};
	fieldsArray[paramName] = label;

	if (arguments.length > 3) {
	fieldsArray.scroll_timing = timing
	MonsterInsightsObject.sendEvent('event', 'scroll_depth', fieldsArray);
	} else {
	MonsterInsightsObject.sendEvent('event', 'scroll_depth', fieldsArray);
	}
			}

		function calculateMarks(docHeight) {
		return {
		'25%' : parseInt(docHeight * 0.25, 10),
		'50%' : parseInt(docHeight * 0.50, 10),
		'75%' : parseInt(docHeight * 0.75, 10),
		/* Cushion to trigger 100% event in iOS */
		'100%': docHeight - 5
		};
		}

		function checkMarks(marks, scrollDistance, timing) {
		/* Check each active mark */
		$.each(marks, function(key, val) {
		if ( $.inArray(key, cache) === -1 && scrollDistance >= val ) {
		sendEvent('Percentage', key, scrollDistance, timing);
		cache.push(key);
		}
		});
		}

		function rounded(scrollDistance) {
		/* Returns String */
		return (Math.floor(scrollDistance/250) * 250).toString();
		}

		function init() {
		bindScrollDepth();
		}

		/*
		* Public Methods
		*/

		/* Reset Scroll Depth with the originally initialized options */
		$.scrollDepth.reset = function() {
		cache = [];
		lastPixelDepth = 0;
		$window.off('scroll.scrollDepth');
		bindScrollDepth();
		};

		/* Add DOM elements to be tracked */
		$.scrollDepth.addElements = function(elems) {

		if (typeof elems == "undefined" || !$.isArray(elems)) {
		return;
		}

		$.merge(options.elements, elems);

		/* If scroll event has been unbound from window, rebind */
		if (!scrollEventBound) {
		bindScrollDepth();
		}

		};

		/* Remove DOM elements currently tracked */
		$.scrollDepth.removeElements = function(elems) {

		if (typeof elems == "undefined" || !$.isArray(elems)) {
		return;
		}

		$.each(elems, function(index, elem) {

		var inElementsArray = $.inArray(elem, options.elements);
		var inCacheArray = $.inArray(elem, cache);

		if (inElementsArray != -1) {
		options.elements.splice(inElementsArray, 1);
		}

		if (inCacheArray != -1) {
		cache.splice(inCacheArray, 1);
		}

		});

		};

		/*
		* Throttle function borrowed from:
		* Underscore.js 1.5.2
		* https://underscorejs.org
		* (c) 2009-2013 Jeremy Ashkenas, DocumentCloud and Investigative Reporters & Editors
		* Underscore may be freely distributed under the MIT license.
		*/

		function throttle(func, wait) {
		var context, args, result;
		var timeout = null;
		var previous = 0;
		var later = function() {
		previous = new Date;
		timeout = null;
		result = func.apply(context, args);
		};
		return function() {
		var now = new Date;
		if (!previous) previous = now;
		var remaining = wait - (now - previous);
		context = this;
		args = arguments;
		if (remaining <= 0) {
		clearTimeout(timeout);
		timeout = null;
		previous = now;
		result = func.apply(context, args);
		} else if (!timeout) {
		timeout = setTimeout(later, remaining);
		}
		return result;
		};
		}

		/*
		* Scroll Event
		*/

		function bindScrollDepth() {

		scrollEventBound = true;

		$window.on('scroll.scrollDepth', throttle(function() {
		/*
		* We calculate document and window height on each scroll event to
		* account for dynamic DOM changes.
		*/

		var docHeight = $(document).height(),
		winHeight = window.innerHeight ? window.innerHeight : $window.height(),
		scrollDistance = $window.scrollTop() + winHeight,

		/* Recalculate percentage marks */
		marks = calculateMarks(docHeight),

		/* Timing */
		timing = +new Date - startTime;

		checkMarks(marks, scrollDistance, timing);
		}, 500));

		}

		init();
		};

		/* UMD export */
		return $.scrollDepth;

		}));

		jQuery.scrollDepth();
		} else {
		setTimeout(monsterinsights_scroll_tracking_load, 200);
		}
		}
		monsterinsights_scroll_tracking_load();
		});
		}
		/* End MonsterInsights Scroll Tracking */
			/* MonsterInsights Conversion Event */
	jQuery(document).ready(function() {
		jQuery('a[data-mi-conversion-event]')
			.off('click.monsterinsightsConversion')
			.on('click.monsterinsightsConversion', function() {
				if ( typeof(__gtagTracker) !== 'undefined' && __gtagTracker ) {
					var $link = jQuery(this);
					var eventName = $link.attr('data-mi-event-name');
					if ( typeof eventName === 'undefined' || ! eventName ) {
						// Fallback to first word of the <a> tag, lowercase, strip html
						var text = $link.text().trim();
						text = text.replace(/(<([^>]+)>)/gi, '').toLowerCase();
						var firstWord = text.split(/\s+/)[0] || '';

						if ( firstWord ) {
							eventName = 'click-' + firstWord;
						} else {
							eventName = $link.parent().hasClass('wp-block-image') ? 'image-click' : 'button-click';
						}
					}
					__gtagTracker('event', 'mi-' + eventName);
				}
			});
	});
	/* End MonsterInsights Conversion Event */
